## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / mathematical biology (population dynamics)
**Analysis**: The variables t (time), P (population size), and target dP_dt (population growth rate) indicate a continuous-time population dynamics model where growth depends on current abundance and possibly explicit time forcing (seasonality or changing environment). Typical structures express dP_dt as P times a per-capita growth function of P and/or t, often with density dependence, Allee effects, or harvesting/immigration terms.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Malthusian (exponential) growth ODE: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited resources; constant per-capita growth)
- Constant net flow (immigration/emigration): dP_dt = c0 + c1 * P (baseline inflow plus proportional growth/decline)
- Logistic growth ODE (Verhulst): dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**2 (linear density dependence; carrying capacity emerges as c0/c1)
- Theta-logistic (generalized density dependence): dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**(c2 + 1) (nonlinear crowding; flexible approach to carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth ODE: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (per-capita growth declines ~ log(P); asymmetric sigmoidal trajectories)
- Richards-type form (flexible logistic family): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (tunable sigmoidal shape via exponent c2)
- Allee effect (cubic density dependence): dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (low-density suppression with possible bistability)
- Strong Allee (factored form): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (c2 - P) (growth only between an Allee threshold and an upper limit)
- Saturating (crowding-limited) per-capita growth: dP_dt = c0 * P / (P + c1) - c2 * P (resource-limited recruitment with linear mortality)
- Constant-yield harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**2 - c2 (logistic growth with constant removal/harvest)
- Saturating harvest (Type II): dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**2 - c2 * P / (P + c3) (harvest/predation saturates at high P)
- Seasonal forcing of growth rate: dP_dt = P * (c0 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) - c3 * P**2 (periodic environment affecting per-capita growth)
- Time-varying carrying capacity (environmental change): dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * exp(c2 * t) * P**2 (crowding term strengthens/weakens exponentially over time)
- Per-capita polynomial model: dP_dt = P * (c0 + c1 * P + c2 * P**2) (generic continuous-time density dependence fitted from data)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Factorization by P (i.e., dP_dt = P * g(P,t)) often reflects births and deaths scaling with the number of individuals; check whether dP_dt/P collapses onto a simpler function of P or t.
- A negative quadratic term in P (… - c * P**2) is a hallmark of pairwise competition/crowding; it typically produces a stable carrying capacity.
- A log(c/P) term implies Gompertz-type regulation: per-capita growth decreases approximately linearly with log(P), giving asymmetric sigmoidal growth curves.
- Higher-than-quadratic powers in P (e.g., -c * P**(1+theta)) indicate nonlinear density dependence; stronger crowding at high P changes how sharply growth slows near carrying capacity.
- A cubic or factored form with (P - threshold) suggests an Allee effect: negative growth at low P and possible bistability/critical population thresholds.
- An additive constant term in dP_dt (±c0) suggests external inputs/outputs (immigration, stocking, constant harvesting) that do not scale with P.
- Rational terms like P/(P + c) indicate saturating processes (limited resources, saturating predation/harvest) and tend to flatten rates at high P.
- Sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) terms signal seasonal forcing; multiplying by P typically means seasonality acts on per-capita growth rather than absolute inflow.
- Explicit exp(c*t) multiplying growth or competition terms signals long-term environmental change (trend in productivity, mortality, or carrying capacity) rather than intrinsic density feedback.

GT Equivalence Verification (BPG2)
============================================================
GT: c0*P*sin(c1*t) + c2*P*exp(-c3*t)
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function (for all real t, P):
\[
F(t,P)=0.2569297861\,P\sin(0.7218439643\,t)+0.1149290460\,P e^{-0.03038461977\,t}.
\]
Key structural facts:
- GT is **linear in \(P\)** (overall factor \(P\)).
- GT has **no \(P^2\)**, no \(\frac{1}{P+\cdot}\), no \(|P|\), no Max/Abs, no logs.
- GT’s \(t\)-dependence is exactly a **single sine term** plus a **single decaying exponential**, both multiplied by \(P\).
So any candidate must be able (by parameter choices) to reduce to \(P\cdot(A\sin(\omega t)+B e^{-kt})\) with no extra terms.

Now check each candidate.

1) \(P^2 c0 + Pc1 + Pc2\sin(c3 t+c4)+c5 t+c6+\frac{c7}{c8 t+c9}\).  
Has \(P^2\) unless \(c0=0\). Also has \(Pc1\) (can set \(c1=0\)), and non-\(P\) terms \(c5 t,c6,\) rational-in-\(t\) (set \(c5=c6=c7=0\)). Then it becomes \(P c2\sin(c3 t+c4)\) only: **cannot create \(P e^{-kt}\)**. No match.

2) Similar to (1) but has \(c7 e^{c8 t}/P^5\). To avoid nonlinearity in \(P\), must set \(c7=0\). Then reduces to sine + affine terms only, still no \(P e^{-kt}\). No match.

3) Like (1) without rational term. Can reduce to sine only; cannot produce exponential. No match.

4) Contains \(P^2 c0\) (must set \(c0=0\)) and a nonlinear rational-in-\(P\) term \(P\cdot P^{c1}c2/(P^{c1}+c3)\) (must kill it by \(c2=0\) to keep linear-in-\(P\)). Then it’s \(P c4 + P c5\sin(\cdot)+c8+c9 t\); can zero constants, leaving sine only. No exponential. No match.

5) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ P c4/(P+c5)+P c6 + c7|P|+c8\).  
To match GT (linear in \(P\) with no \(|P|\) and no rational-in-\(P\)), need \(c7=0\) and \(c4=0\). Then it’s \(P(\text{constant}+\sin)+c8\). Set constant and \(c8\) to 0 leaves sine only. No exponential. No match.

6) \(P c0\sin(\cdot)+ P c3/(P+c4)+P c5 + P + c6 + c7\max(0,-P+c8)\).  
Must remove max term: \(c7=0\). Remove rational: \(c3=0\). Then have \(P c0\sin(\cdot)+P c5 + P + c6\). Can zero constants, leaving sine only. No exponential. No match.

7) Same issue as (5) without Abs: must set rational term to 0; then only sine + constants. No exponential. No match.

8) Like (7) plus Max term; must set Max coefficient 0; still no exponential. No match.

9) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ c4 t + c5 + \frac{c6}{c7 t+c8}\).  
Non-\(P\) terms must be zeroed: \(c4=c5=c6=0\). Then only \(P(\text{const}+\sin)\). No exponential. No match.

10) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+P c4 + c5 + c6 t + \frac{c7}{c8+t}\).  
Zero non-GT terms -> sine + \(P\) constant only. No exponential. No match.

11) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ c4(c5+t)^{c6}\).  
Must kill the non-\(P\) power term: \(c4=0\). Then sine + \(P\) constant only. No exponential. No match.

12) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+P c4 + c5 + c6/t + c7/(c8 t+c9)\).  
Must set \(c5=c6=c7=0\). Then sine + \(P\) constant only. No exponential. No match.

13) Same as (12) with \(c7/(c8+t)\). Same conclusion. No match.

14) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ c4/t + c5 + c6/(c7 t+c8)\).  
Must kill non-\(P\) terms: \(c4=c5=c6=0\). Then sine + \(P\) constant only. No exponential. No match.

15) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ P c4/t + c5 + c6/(c7 t+c8)\).  
To avoid \(P/t\) and non-\(P\) rational: set \(c4=c5=c6=0\). Then sine + \(P\) constant only. No exponential. No match.

16) \(P c0 + P c1/(P+c2) + c3 e^{c4 t} + c5 + c6\log(P c7+1)\sin(\cdot)\).  
GT has \(P e^{-kt}\), but here exponential term is **not multiplied by \(P\)**. If we try to force it: cannot, since \(c3 e^{c4 t}\) lacks \(P\). Also has log(P) term unless \(c6=0\), and rational-in-\(P\) unless \(c1=0\). After zeroing, still exponential not times \(P\). No match.

17) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ P c4(c5+t)^{c6}\).  
The extra \(P\cdot (c5+t)^{c6}\) cannot equal \(P e^{-kt}\) for all \(t\) (power vs exponential), unless \(c4=0\). Then only sine + constant. No match.

18) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ P c4/(c5 t+c6) + c7 + c8/(c5 t+c6)\).  
GT has no \(1/(at+b)\) terms; must set \(c4=c8=0\) and \(c7=0\). Then sine + \(P\) constant only. No exponential. No match.

19) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ P c4 + P c5/(c6 t+c7) + c8 + c9/(c6 t+c7)\).  
Must kill \(1/(at+b)\) terms: \(c5=c9=0\), and constants \(c8=0\). Then sine + \(P\) constant only. No exponential. No match.

20) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ P c4(c5+t)^{c6} + c7\).  
As in (17): power term can’t become exponential; must set \(c4=0\), then no exponential. No match.

21) \(P\cdot P^{c0}c1/(P^{c0}+c2) + P c3 + P c4 + P c5\sin(\cdot)+c8+c9 t\).  
To keep linear in \(P\), must remove the nonlinear rational-in-\(P\) term (set \(c1=0\)). Then only sine + \(P\) constants + affine-in-\(t\) constants; no exponential. No match.

22) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ P c4/(c5 t+c6) + c7/t + c8\).  
\(P/(at+b)\) and \(1/t\) must be removed: set \(c4=c7=0\), \(c8=0\). Then sine + \(P\) constant only. No exponential. No match.

23) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ c4 e^{P c5} + c6 e^{c7 t} + c8\).  
Has \(e^{P c5}\) (must set \(c4=0\) or \(c5=0\) but then it’s constant). Also \(c6 e^{c7 t}\) is not multiplied by \(P\), so cannot match \(P e^{-kt}\). No match.

24) \(P c0 + P c1/(P+c2) + c3\sin(\cdot)+ c6 + c7\sin(\cdot)\).  
Sine terms are not necessarily multiplied by \(P\); GT requires the sine term be \(P\)-scaled. To avoid non-\(P\) sines, set \(c3=c7=0\). Then no \(P\)-sine at all. Also no \(P\)-exponential. No match.

25) Logs/exponentials in \(P\); structure totally different from \(P\sin + P e^{-kt}\). No match.

26) \(P c0\sin(\cdot)+ P c3/(P+c4)+ P c5(c6+t)^{c7}+ P + c8\).  
Must kill rational-in-\(P\): \(c3=0\). Power term cannot become exponential; set \(c5=0\). Then only \(P\sin\) plus \(P\) constant. No exponential. No match.

27) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ c4 e^{c5 t} + c6\).  
Exponential term is not multiplied by \(P\). If set \(c4=0\), lose exponential. No match.

28) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ P c4 + c5 + c6\max(0,-P+c7)\).  
Must set \(c6=0\), \(c5=0\). Then sine + \(P\) constant only. No exponential. No match.

29) \(P c0/(P+c1) + c2 e^{c3 t} + c4 + c5\log(P c6+1)\sin(\cdot)\).  
Nonlinear in \(P\) unless \(c0=0\) and \(c5=0\). Then exponential term still not multiplied by \(P\). No match.

30) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ P c4 + c5/(P+c6)+ c7|P|+c8\).  
Must set \(c5=0\), \(c7=0\), \(c8=0\). Then sine + \(P\) constant only. No exponential. No match.

31) \(P^2 c0 e^{c1 t} + P c2 + P c3/(P+c4) + c5 + c6\sin(\cdot)\).  
To avoid \(P^2\): set \(c0=0\). Then sine term is not multiplied by \(P\) (it’s \(c6\sin\)), so must set \(c6=0\) to avoid mismatch; then no \(P\)-sine. No \(P\)-exponential. No match.

32) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ c4 e^{c5 t} + c6 e^{c7 t} + c8\).  
Exponentials not multiplied by \(P\). No match.

33) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ P c4 e^{c5 t} + c6 e^{c7 t} + c8\).  
Has a \(P\cdot e^{c5 t}\) term, which could match GT’s \(P e^{-k t}\) by choosing \(c5=-0.0303846\) and \(c4=0.1149290460\).  
But there is also an extra non-\(P\) exponential \(c6 e^{c7 t}\) and constant \(c8\). We can set \(c6=0\) and \(c8=0\).  
Then candidate becomes:
\[
P c0 + P c1\sin(c2 t+c3) + P c4 e^{c5 t}.
\]
GT has **no pure \(P\) constant term**, so set \(c0=0\).  
Now match sine: need \(c1=0.2569297861\), \(c2=0.7218439643\), and phase \(c3=0\) (or any \(2\pi k\)).  
Match exponential: \(c4=0.1149290460\), \(c5=-0.03038461977\).  
This exactly reproduces GT for all \(t,P\). **Match found.**

34) \(P c0 + P c1\sin(\cdot)+ P c4 + c5 + c6/(c7 t+c8)\).  
No exponential; rational term must be zeroed; then sine + \(P\) constant only. No match.

35) Includes Max(0,P+c5) and a non-\(P\) exponential; cannot match. No match.

36) Has \(1/(c7 t+c8)\) and \(1/t\); no exponential. No match.

37) Has non-\(P\) rational terms including \(1/(c7 e^{c8 t}+1)\) (logistic-like), not \(P e^{-kt}\). No match.

38) Has \(P/t\) and non-\(P\) sine; cannot become GT. No match.

39) Has rational-in-\(P\) and also a non-\(P\) sine term; cannot reduce to GT without killing needed sine. No match.

40) Has rational-in-\(P\), \(P^{c3} e^{c5 t}\) etc; to get linear in \(P\) would require \(c3=1\) and also remove rational and extra sine; but still includes an extra non-\(P\) sine term. Cannot match exactly. No match.

41) Sine not multiplied by \(P\) and has \(1/t\) terms. No match.

42) Sines not multiplied by \(P\), plus rational-in-\(P\). No match.

43) Has \(P^2\) and non-\(P\) sine and \(e^{t}/P^5\). Cannot match. No match.

44) Has \(\sin(P c4 + c5)\) (sine depends on \(P\)), incompatible with GT. No match.

45) Only one sine and constants; no \(P\)-exponential. No match.

46) Has extra non-\(P\) sine term \(c5\sin(\cdot)\) and \(P^2\) etc; cannot match GT exactly. No match.

47) Sine terms not multiplied by \(P\). No match.

48) Has \(P\cdot P^{c0}c1\) (generally \(P^{c0+1}\)), plus non-\(P\) sine. Not match.

49) Has \(P^{c3}c4\) term; to be linear need \(c3=1\) but then it’s just \(P c4\) (constant in \(t\)), no exponential. No match.

50) Has \(P c0/(P+c1)\) nonlinear in \(P\) and non-\(P\) sines. No match.

Therefore only candidate 33 can be parameterized to equal the GT for all \(t,P\).
